Question : 1. Present Simple Tense

Used to express daily activities, regular action, facts, timetable. Something that always/often do.
Rules :
S + V1
Example :
I brush my teeth
He works at the office
She goes to school
They leave the hospital (not regular action, unless, they're working in hospital)
You learn German
She gets up at 9 AM
The plane leaves in 1 hour 
They like tea
----
to be (am, is, are) are not used in present simple if there's a verb
+ing ending also isn't used in this tense.
-----
"She is pretty"
if you use noun or adjective you need to be (am, is, are) 
I'm here
She is in the park 
They are outside
